<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> (145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>because
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziek.html>ziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not coming <b>because</b> he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sick.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word order <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> subject-object-verb after <i><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></i>. Synonyms, like want differ only by this.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">omertà</i>, from a Southern dialectal rhotacist variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">umiltà</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">humility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">humilitās</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">humilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">humble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:humus.html>humus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ground, soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omerta.html>omerta</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omerta.html>omertas</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omerta.html>omertaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">crime</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">omertà</span>, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">extensively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">wall of silence</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">code of silence</span></li></ol>

***omgang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:omgang.html>omgang</a> (13461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ommegang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*umbigang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*umbigangaz</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">around</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">course, way</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omgang.html>omgang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omgangen.html>omgangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omgang.html>omgangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">contact</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">march</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <span class="Latn" lang="en">procession</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gallery</span> around a <span class="Latn" lang="en">tower</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">relationship</span> (family, sexual etc...)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:omgang.html>omgang</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<ol><li>to surround
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Amazonebekken <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:omgeven.html>omgeven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogland.html>Hoogland</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Guyana in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>noorden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andes.html>Andes</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:westen.html>westen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogland.html>Hoogland</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Brazilië in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuiden.html>zuiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oosten.html>oosten</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amazonebekken">[1]</a></sup>  |  The Amazon basin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> surrounded by the Guyana Highlands to the north, the <a href = vnd.unilang:andes.html>Andes</a> to the west and the Brazilian Highlands to the south and east.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">omission</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">omittere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Post-classical Latin introduced the term from the past participial <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">omittere</i> and the suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omissie.html>omissie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omissie.html>omissies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omissie.html>omissietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">omission</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">negligence</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">omitteren</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:omissie.html>omissie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

<p>From <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omkeren.html>omkeren</a></span>. ***omkomen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:omkomen.html>omkomen</a> (9494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ommecomen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pass by, end, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">umbekomen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pass by, end, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">umkommen</i>. Compare the phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>, and further <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ombrengen.html>ombrengen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>Regarding</a> the broader semantic use in both Middle Dutch and Middle High German, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not certain that the short verbs are <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> ellipses of the phrases with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i>, though they have without doubt <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by them.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omkomen.html>omkomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to perish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:omstandig.html>omstandig</a> (80946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">around</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
